*** COMPREHENSIVE AEROLOGICAL REFERENCE DATASET (CARDS) STATION HISTORY *** 

NUMBER = STATION NUMBER (1ST 5 DIGITS IS WMO NUMBER)
NAME = STATION NAME 
COUNTRY = FIPS COUNTRY CODE 
LATITUDE = LATITUDE IN DEGREES & HUNDREDTHS (SOUTH = NEGATIVE)  
LONGITUDE = LONGITUDE IN DEGREES & HUNDREDTHS (WEST = NEGATIVE) 
ELEV = ELEVATION IN METERS (UNKNOWN = 9999.9)   
BEGINS = BEGINNING YEAR-MONTH FOR DIGITAL DATA  
ENDS = ENDING YEAR-MONTH FOR DIGITAL DATA (999912 = STATION STILL ACTIVE)
